 The State Bank of India has drastically reduced the fees levied on electronic transactions to encourage internet banking and mobile banking
 digital bhugtan ko badhaava dene ke liye saarvajanik kshetra ke pramukh bank bhartiya state bank (esbiai) ne enift or artijies ke jariye electranik tareeke se dhan hastantaran shulk main 75 pratishat tak katautee kii he
 This reduction in charges will be applicable from Saturday
 bank ne ek bayaan main kaha he ki isse uske 5
 27 crore customers will benefit
 bayaan main kaha gaya he ki shulkon main yah katautee bank dwaara di ja rahi internet banking (aienbi) or mobile banking (embi) sevaaon ke jariye kiye jane vaale lenden par lagu hogi
 This fee deduction of the bank will be applicable from July 15
 iske liye bank ne sanshodhit enift or artijies shulk jari kiye hai
 As per the revised charges, NEFT fee has been reduced from two to one rupee on transfer of funds up to Rs 10,000
 ek lakh rupee tak ke hastantaran par do rupee kaa shulk lagegaa
 Similarly, NEFT duty on transfer from one to two lakh rupees has been reduced from the current 12 rupees to three rupees
 vahiin do lakh rupee se adhik ke kosh hastantaran par yah shulk paanch rupee hoga
 So far it was 20 rupees
 artijies lenden ke liye do lakh rupee se paanch lakh rupee ke hastantaran ke liye shulk paanch rupee hoga
 Till now the bank charges Rs 20 for such transactions
 yadi graahak artijies ke jariye paanch lakh rupee se adhik kaa hastantaran karata he to us par 10 rupee kaa shulk lagegaa, jo abhi tak 40 rupee he
 If funds are transferred through executives at bank branches, then the tariff rates will vary
 sabhi nae shulkon par 18 pratishat kii dar se jiesti lagegaa
 Along with this, SBI has abolished fees on transfer of up to Rs 1,000 through instant payment service (IMPS)
 tippaniyan SBI Managing Director Rajneesh Kumar said, "as part of our strategy and the Government of India's Digital Economy initiative, we have reduced charges on NEFT and RTGS transactions to encourage Internet banking and mobile banking
" march ke ant tak esbiai ke internet banking graahakon kii sankhya 3
 27 crore and the number of mobile banking customers was 20 million
 esbiai duniya ke sheersh 50 bainkon main shaamil he
 It is the largest commercial bank in the country in terms of assets, deposits, profits, branches and employees
 (input agenciyon se) The statement said that this reduction in charges would apply to transactions carried out by the bank through Internet banking (INB) and mobile banking (MB) services
 bank kii yah shulk katautee 15 july se lagu hogi

 sanshodhit shulkon ke anusaar 10,000 rupee tak ke kosh ke hastantaran par enift shulk do se ghataakar ek rupee kar diya gaya he

 abhi tak yah 20 rupee tha
